# I-cd-567 — STRUCTURAL GATE FIX (Codex consult verdict 2026-05-20)

## Verdict: Option D (operator-held admin) + auto-merge-on-green

### INTERIM RULE (effective immediately, until Option D is live)
**Claude STOPS auto-merging. Queue every PR for operator merge.** The
SHA-pinned codex_diff discipline is review EVIDENCE, not merge permission.
The #709 incident proves soft enforcement is not the control boundary.

### Claude can do (engineering, queued for operator merge)
- PR mirroring codex-required.yml + codex_artifact_gate.yml onto `main` (default branch) so Actions registers them.
- Stable unique job/check names.
- CODEOWNERS / ruleset files via PR.

### Operator MUST do (admin — Claude cannot + must not)
- Remove Admin/Maintain/bypass from sotaleung-wec + aldrinor (drop to Write/Triage).
- Apply polaris branch protection: required checks bound to the GitHub Actions App app_id (not bare contexts — Claude must not be able to set commit statuses), enforce/no-bypass ON, required PR review, required conversation resolution.
- Hold the ONLY admin token; revoke/replace Claude tokens with non-admin, non-workflow-write.
- Enable auto-merge (so green codex-required auto-merges without Claude bypassing).

### Why
enforce_admins=false + Claude holding the aldrinor admin token = the
agent-as-execution-engine + agent-as-certification-oracle anti-pattern
(the 28-commits failure). Codex review is currently honored only because
Claude chooses to. Not structural until Claude cannot bypass OR alter
branch protection.

---

## MERGE-AUTHORITY PROTOCOL (Codex decision 2026-05-20, operator-directed)

**DECISION: "Codex decides → Claude executes → operator owns" is ACCEPTED as an INTERIM bridge.** Permanent design is still Option D (operator admin lockdown). It breaks the dangerous coupling (Claude no longer certifies its OWN merge — Codex does) but is not a hard boundary while Claude holds an admin-capable token.

### Claude may merge a PR ONLY when ALL hold:
1. **Codex explicitly authorized** — final decision says `MERGE AUTHORIZED`; BOTH brief + diff tracks APPROVE; approval is for the exact committed head SHA + base.
2. **Canonical diff integrity** — codex_diff.patch exists; its canonical-diff-sha256 matches the actual PR diff; head SHA unchanged since approval. Any mismatch/regenerate/force-push VOIDS approval.
3. **Required CI green** — codex-required SUCCESSFUL, not merely present. Failing/skipped/cancelled/pending/missing/stale BLOCKS. No admin bypass around red/absent checks.
4. **No unresolved blockers** — no Codex REJECT/BLOCK/must-fix; no conflicts; no signing/provenance failure; no unreviewed commits after approval.
5. **Claude posts the decision verbatim in the PR before merging** — PR#, head SHA, base, canonical diff SHA, CI state, exact Codex decision text.
6. **Ordinary auditable merge** — normal merge method; no force-push/history-rewrite/branch-swap/manual-patch; if mechanics need admin bypass → BLOCKED, operator-only.

### OPERATOR-ONLY exclusion list (Claude may NEVER merge, even on Codex APPROVE):
- branch protection / rulesets / permissions / deploy keys / app+token config
- `.github/workflows/**` / CI policy / required-check defs / merge automation
- `CODEOWNERS` / ownership / approval routing
- `polaris-controls/**` / governance / control-plane
- auth / authz / signing keys / secrets / tokens / credentials
- release signing / provenance / attestation / publishing / deploy authority
- anything granting Claude/automation/CI broader write/admin
- emergency/security changes where bypass pressure is part of the ask
- any Claude-authored PR modifying the rules governing Claude's own authority

### #709 would have been BLOCKED under this protocol
(codex-required was RED + SHA mismatch + no verbatim decision posted). The protocol's preconditions 2+3+5 each independently catch it.

tests\fixtures\subagent_prompts\section_writer_response.txt:5:Weight reduction is the most consistently observed outcome across IF trials, and it is mechanistically central to the improvement of insulin resistance in T2DM. In adults with overweight or obesity, IF reduced fat mass by a mean difference of −0.72 kg compared with a non-intervention diet [CITE:ev_243de27dc515c169]. When IF is combined with structured physical exercise, the weight reduction relative to a control diet plus exercise reaches a weighted mean difference of −1.83 kg (P = 0.001) [CITE:ev_749f00cb5c5eea28], suggesting an additive effect when caloric timing is paired with energy expenditure. The largest effect size is observed with modified alternate-day fasting, which produced a weight reduction of −5.18 kg (95% CI: −7.04 to −3.32) compared with a usual diet, supported by high certainty of evidence [CITE:ev_e7bdb4797d3f6f0f]. The differential between these protocols is clinically meaningful: a five-kilogram loss falls within the range associated with measurable improvements in HbA1c and insulin sensitivity, whereas sub-kilogram fat-mass reductions, although statistically significant, may yield more modest glycemic benefits.
tests\fixtures\subagent_prompts\section_writer_response.txt:11:The lipid response to IF reinforces its cardiometabolic relevance for the T2DM population, where dyslipidemia is a frequent comorbidity. Across umbrella-review syntheses, IF reduced low-density lipoprotein cholesterol by a standardized mean difference of −0.20 (95% CI: −0.38 to −0.02; p = 0.027) compared with a non-intervention diet [CITE:ev_410655e66705beb6]. When IF is combined with exercise, the reduction is larger and reported in absolute units: a weighted mean difference of −5.35 mg/dL (P = 0.03) for LDL cholesterol [CITE:ev_39b4891376876856]. Triacylglycerols also fall under IF protocols, with a standardized mean difference of −0.23 (95% CI: −0.39 to −0.06; p = 0.007) [CITE:ev_e273c28dab55ecd8]. The convergence of LDL and triglyceride reductions is consistent with the broader observation that IF exerts beneficial effects on the lipid profile [CITE:ev_dde1177bb61ef9e9], a finding that strengthens its candidacy as an adjunctive intervention for individuals with T2DM whose treatment goals extend beyond glycemic control to encompass cardiovascular risk attenuation.

+"""I-cd-680 — bridge a real pipeline-A artifact_dir to a typed EvidenceContract.
+
+Reuses `build_slice_chain` (I-arch-001d, the same path `GET /runs/{id}/
+bundle.tar.gz` already proves on real runs) and maps the slice-chain into the
+`EvidenceContract` v1.0 schema that the follow-up (#542) and compare (#543)
+endpoints consume.
+
+Scope (Codex Option B, 2026-05-20): real-run RESOLUTION only. We do NOT
+synthesize rich source-document char offsets — pipeline-A does not record
+them. `SourceSpan.span_start`/`span_end` are the truthful 0..len(span_text)
+offsets of the recorded evidence text within ITSELF (the recorded quote IS
+the span). Rich offsets into the original source body are the deferred
+Phase-2 capability (#710), NOT fabricated here (LAW II).
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import json
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any
+
+from polaris_v6.api.artifact_to_slice_chain import build_slice_chain
+from polaris_v6.schemas.evidence_contract import (
+    ContradictionRecord,
+    EvidenceContract,
+    SourceSpan,
+    VerifiedSentence,
+)
+
+
+def _read_contradictions(artifact_dir: Path) -> list[ContradictionRecord]:
+    """Load contradictions.json if present. Real pipeline-A runs write a list
+    of contradiction records; absent/empty → no contradictions."""
+    path = artifact_dir / "contradictions.json"
+    if not path.exists():
+        return []
+    try:
+        raw = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
+    except (json.JSONDecodeError, OSError):
+        return []
+    records: list[ContradictionRecord] = []
+    items = raw if isinstance(raw, list) else raw.get("contradictions", [])
+    for i, item in enumerate(items if isinstance(items, list) else []):
+        if not isinstance(item, dict):
+            continue
+        # Codex iter-1 P2: real pipeline-A clusters use a `claims` list +
+        # `evidence` list rather than claim_a/claim_b/evidence_a/evidence_b.
+        # Map both shapes so real-run contradictions aren't blanked out.
+        claims = item.get("claims")
+        if isinstance(claims, list) and len(claims) >= 2:
+            claim_a, claim_b = str(claims[0]), str(claims[1])
+        else:
+            claim_a, claim_b = str(item.get("claim_a") or ""), str(item.get("claim_b") or "")
+        ev = item.get("evidence")
+        if isinstance(ev, list) and not item.get("evidence_a"):
+            # A flat evidence list — attribute it to side A (best available).
+            evidence_a = [str(x) for x in ev]
+            evidence_b: list[str] = []
+        else:
+            evidence_a = [str(x) for x in (item.get("evidence_a") or [])]
+            evidence_b = [str(x) for x in (item.get("evidence_b") or [])]
+        try:
+            records.append(
+                ContradictionRecord(
+                    contradiction_id=str(item.get("contradiction_id") or item.get("id") or f"c{i}"),
+                    section_id=str(item.get("section_id") or "unknown"),
+                    claim_a=claim_a,
+                    claim_b=claim_b,
+                    evidence_a=evidence_a,
+                    evidence_b=evidence_b,
+                    resolution=item.get("resolution")
+                    if item.get("resolution")
+                    in ("unresolved", "claim_a_preferred", "claim_b_preferred", "noted_both")
+                    else "noted_both",
+                )
+            )
+        except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — a malformed record is skipped, not fatal
+            continue
+    return records
+
+
+def build_evidence_contract_from_artifact(
+    artifact_dir: Path,
+    *,
+    run_id: str,
+    template: str,
+    question: str,
+    queued_at: str,
+    finished_at: str,
+    pipeline_status: str,
+) -> EvidenceContract:
+    """Synthesize a fully-valid EvidenceContract from a REAL artifact_dir.
+
+    Run metadata (run_id/template/question/timestamps/status) is supplied by
+    the caller from run_store (the authoritative source); the evidence + the
+    verified sentences come from the slice-chain.
+
+    Raises FileNotFoundError / SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError from
+    build_slice_chain — the caller maps these to 404 / 422.
+    """
+    _decision, pool, report = build_slice_chain(artifact_dir)
+
+    evidence_pool: list[SourceSpan] = []
+    for src in pool.sources:
+        # The recorded evidence text. build_slice_chain only admits T1
+        # legal-cleared sources, so source_tier is within SourceSpan's
+        # T1/T2/T3 Literal.
+        span_text = src.full_text or src.snippet or src.title or "n/a"
+        evidence_pool.append(
+            SourceSpan(
+                evidence_id=src.source_id,
+                source_url=str(src.url),
+                source_tier=src.tier.value,
+                # Truthful self-offset of the recorded span; rich
+                # source-document offsets are deferred to #710.
+                span_start=0,
+                span_end=len(span_text),
+                span_text=span_text,
+            )
+        )
+
+    verified_sentences: list[VerifiedSentence] = []
+    for section in report.sections:
+        for sent in section.verified_sentences:
+            verified_sentences.append(
+                VerifiedSentence(
+                    section_id=sent.section_id,
+                    sentence_text=sent.sentence_text,
+                    provenance_tokens=list(sent.provenance_tokens),
+                    # The slice-chain records a single verifier_pass (Local AND
+                    # Global must both hold for a sentence to pass strict_verify),
+                    # so it maps to both EvidenceContract flags.
+                    verifier_local_pass=sent.verifier_pass,
+                    verifier_global_pass=sent.verifier_pass,
+                    drop_reason=sent.drop_reason,
+                )
+            )
+
+    return EvidenceContract(
+        run_id=run_id,
+        template=template,
+        question=question,
+        queued_at=queued_at,
+        finished_at=finished_at,
+        pipeline_status=pipeline_status,
+        evidence_pool=evidence_pool,
+        verified_sentences=verified_sentences,
+        frame_coverage=[],
+        contradictions=_read_contradictions(artifact_dir),
+        cost_usd=float(report.cost_usd or 0.0),
+        generator_model=report.generator_model,
+        verifier_model=report.evaluator_model,
+        family_segregation_passed=report.family_segregation_passed,
+    )

 114:             detail=f"Run {run_id!r} manifest.json missing or invalid: {exc}",
 115:         ) from exc
 116:     if not manifest_raw.get("release_allowed", False):
 117:         raise HTTPException(
 118:             status_code=422,
 119:             detail=(
 120:                 f"Run {run_id!r} is release-blocked "
 121:                 f"(pipeline_status={run.pipeline_status!r}, release_allowed=False); "
 122:                 f"EvidenceContract cannot ship until the release gate clears."
 123:             ),
 124:         )
 125: 
 126:     try:
 127:         return build_evidence_contract_from_artifact(
 128:             artifact_dir,
 129:             run_id=run.run_id,
 130:             template=run.template or "custom",
 131:             question=run.question or "",
 132:             queued_at=str(run.queued_at or ""),
 133:             finished_at=str(run.finished_at or ""),
 134:             pipeline_status=run.pipeline_status or "success",
 135:         )
 136:     except SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError as exc:
 137:         raise HTTPException(
 138:             status_code=422,
 139:             detail=f"Run {run_id!r} has no shippable sections after the "
 140:             f"sovereignty cascade: {exc}",
 141:         ) from exc
 142:     except FileNotFoundError as exc:
 143:         raise HTTPException(
 144:             status_code=404,
 145:             detail=f"Run {run_id!r} artifact_dir is missing required files: {exc}",
 146:         ) from exc
 147: 
 148: 
 149: @router.get("/{run_id}/bundle", response_model=EvidenceContract)
 150: def get_bundle(run_id: str) -> EvidenceContract:
 151:     # I-cd-680: real runs now resolve to a typed EvidenceContract built from
 152:     # the slice-chain (was 404-with-pointer-to-bundle.tar.gz). Golden
 153:     # fixtures unchanged.
 154:     return load_evidence_contract_for_run(run_id)
 155: 
 156: 
 157: @router.get("/{run_id}/bundle.tar.gz")
 158: def get_run_bundle_targz(
 159:     run_id: str,
 160:     sign_fn=Depends(get_sign_fn),
 161: ):
 162:     """Resolve run_id → artifact_dir → signed audit bundle (tar.gz).
 163: 
 164:     I-arch-001d Codex diff iter-1 P1-001: `Depends(get_sign_fn)` MUST use
 165:     the actual `get_sign_fn` callable from audit_bundle_route — the
 166:     create_app() registers `app.dependency_overrides[get_sign_fn]` to
 167:     inject the real GPGSigner when POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID is set. A lambda
 168:     Depends would be a different callable; the override would never fire.
 169: 
 170:     Status codes:
 171:         200: bundleable run; returns application/gzip
 172:         404: run not found, not completed, or artifact_dir missing
 173:         422: run aborted (pipeline_status=abort_*) or sovereignty cascade
 174:              emptied the report
 175:         503: GPG signer not configured (POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID unset) — surfaced
 176:              by the inner build_audit_bundle_response when sign_fn is None.
 177:     """
 178:     info = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 179:     if info is None:
 180:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail={"error": "run not found"})
 181:     if info.lifecycle_status != "completed":
 182:         raise HTTPException(
 183:             status_code=404,
 184:             detail={"error": f"run not completed: lifecycle_status={info.lifecycle_status}"},
 185:         )
 186:     if info.pipeline_status and info.pipeline_status.startswith("abort_"):
 187:         raise HTTPException(
 188:             status_code=422,
 189:             detail={"error": f"run aborted: pipeline_status={info.pipeline_status}", "bundleable": False},
 190:         )
 191:     if not info.artifact_dir:
 192:         raise HTTPException(
 193:             status_code=404, detail={"error": "run has no artifact_dir recorded"}
 194:         )
 195: 
 196:     artifact_dir = Path(info.artifact_dir)
 197:     if not artifact_dir.is_dir():
 198:         raise HTTPException(
 199:             status_code=404,
 200:             detail={"error": f"artifact_dir does not exist on disk: {artifact_dir}"},
 201:         )
 202: 
 203:     # I-arch-001d Codex diff iter-2 P1-002 fix: release_allowed gate.
 204:     # The slice-chain pipeline_verdict collapses partial_* into "success",
 205:     # but a release-blocked partial (e.g. partial_evaluator_advisory with
 206:     # release_allowed=false) MUST NOT ship as a clean bundle. Read the raw
 207:     # manifest.release_allowed flag and refuse with 422 when False.
 208:     try:
 209:         manifest_raw = json.loads((artifact_dir / "manifest.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 210:     except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError) as exc:
 211:         raise HTTPException(
 212:             status_code=404,
 213:             detail={"error": f"manifest.json missing or invalid: {exc}"},
 214:         ) from exc
 215:     if not manifest_raw.get("release_allowed", False):
 216:         raise HTTPException(
 217:             status_code=422,
 218:             detail={
 219:                 "error": (
 220:                     f"run release-blocked: pipeline_status={info.pipeline_status!r}, "
 221:                     f"release_allowed=False. Bundle cannot ship until release gate clears."
 222:                 ),
 223:                 "bundleable": False,
 224:                 "pipeline_status": info.pipeline_status,
 225:             },
 226:         )
 227: 
 228:     try:
 229:         decision, pool, report = build_slice_chain(artifact_dir)
 230:     except SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError as exc:
 231:         raise HTTPException(status_code=422, detail={"error": str(exc)}) from exc
 232:     except FileNotFoundError as exc:
 233:         raise HTTPException(
 234:             status_code=404,
 235:             detail={"error": f"artifact_dir incomplete: {exc}"},
 236:         ) from exc
 237: 
 238:     # I-gen-004 (#496): include the run's reasoning trace in the signed
 239:     # bundle when present. Write-through means the file exists for every
 240:     # completed run; it is hashed under content_type=reasoning_trace.
 241:     extra_files: dict[str, tuple[bytes, str]] | None = None
 242:     trace_path = artifact_dir / "reasoning_trace.jsonl"
 243:     if trace_path.is_file():
 244:         extra_files = {
 245:             "reasoning_trace.jsonl": (
 246:                 trace_path.read_bytes(),
 247:                 "reasoning_trace",
 248:             )
 249:         }
 250: 
 251:     return build_audit_bundle_response(
 252:         decision, pool, report, sign_fn, extra_files=extra_files,
 253:     )

 succeeded in 2316ms:
   1: """I-cd-680 — bridge a real pipeline-A artifact_dir to a typed EvidenceContract.
   2: 
   3: Reuses `build_slice_chain` (I-arch-001d, the same path `GET /runs/{id}/
   4: bundle.tar.gz` already proves on real runs) and maps the slice-chain into the
   5: `EvidenceContract` v1.0 schema that the follow-up (#542) and compare (#543)
   6: endpoints consume.
   7: 
   8: Scope (Codex Option B, 2026-05-20): real-run RESOLUTION only. We do NOT
   9: synthesize rich source-document char offsets — pipeline-A does not record
  10: them. `SourceSpan.span_start`/`span_end` are the truthful 0..len(span_text)
  11: offsets of the recorded evidence text within ITSELF (the recorded quote IS
  12: the span). Rich offsets into the original source body are the deferred
  13: Phase-2 capability (#710), NOT fabricated here (LAW II).
  14: """
  15: 
  16: from __future__ import annotations
  17: 
  18: import json
  19: from pathlib import Path
  20: from typing import Any
  21: 
  22: from polaris_v6.api.artifact_to_slice_chain import build_slice_chain
  23: from polaris_v6.schemas.evidence_contract import (
  24:     ContradictionRecord,
  25:     EvidenceContract,
  26:     SourceSpan,
  27:     VerifiedSentence,
  28: )
  29: 
  30: 
  31: def _read_contradictions(artifact_dir: Path) -> list[ContradictionRecord]:
  32:     """Load contradictions.json if present. Real pipeline-A runs write a list
  33:     of contradiction records; absent/empty → no contradictions."""
  34:     path = artifact_dir / "contradictions.json"
  35:     if not path.exists():
  36:         return []
  37:     try:
  38:         raw = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
  39:     except (json.JSONDecodeError, OSError):
  40:         return []
  41:     records: list[ContradictionRecord] = []
  42:     items = raw if isinstance(raw, list) else raw.get("contradictions", [])
  43:     for i, item in enumerate(items if isinstance(items, list) else []):
  44:         if not isinstance(item, dict):
  45:             continue
  46:         # Codex iter-1 P2: real pipeline-A clusters use a `claims` list +
  47:         # `evidence` list rather than claim_a/claim_b/evidence_a/evidence_b.
  48:         # Map both shapes so real-run contradictions aren't blanked out.
  49:         claims = item.get("claims")
  50:         if isinstance(claims, list) and len(claims) >= 2:
  51:             claim_a, claim_b = str(claims[0]), str(claims[1])
  52:         else:
  53:             claim_a, claim_b = str(item.get("claim_a") or ""), str(item.get("claim_b") or "")
  54:         ev = item.get("evidence")
  55:         if isinstance(ev, list) and not item.get("evidence_a"):
  56:             # A flat evidence list — attribute it to side A (best available).
  57:             evidence_a = [str(x) for x in ev]
  58:             evidence_b: list[str] = []
  59:         else:
  60:             evidence_a = [str(x) for x in (item.get("evidence_a") or [])]
  61:             evidence_b = [str(x) for x in (item.get("evidence_b") or [])]
  62:         try:
  63:             records.append(
  64:                 ContradictionRecord(
  65:                     contradiction_id=str(item.get("contradiction_id") or item.get("id") or f"c{i}"),
  66:                     section_id=str(item.get("section_id") or "unknown"),
  67:                     claim_a=claim_a,
  68:                     claim_b=claim_b,
  69:                     evidence_a=evidence_a,
  70:                     evidence_b=evidence_b,
  71:                     resolution=item.get("resolution")
  72:                     if item.get("resolution")
  73:                     in ("unresolved", "claim_a_preferred", "claim_b_preferred", "noted_both")
  74:                     else "noted_both",
  75:                 )
  76:             )
  77:         except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — a malformed record is skipped, not fatal
  78:             continue
  79:     return records
  80: 
  81: 
  82: def build_evidence_contract_from_artifact(
  83:     artifact_dir: Path,
  84:     *,
  85:     run_id: str,
  86:     template: str,
  87:     question: str,
  88:     queued_at: str,
  89:     finished_at: str,
  90:     pipeline_status: str,
  91: ) -> EvidenceContract:
  92:     """Synthesize a fully-valid EvidenceContract from a REAL artifact_dir.
  93: 
  94:     Run metadata (run_id/template/question/timestamps/status) is supplied by
  95:     the caller from run_store (the authoritative source); the evidence + the
  96:     verified sentences come from the slice-chain.
  97: 
  98:     Raises FileNotFoundError / SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError from
  99:     build_slice_chain — the caller maps these to 404 / 422.
 100:     """
 101:     _decision, pool, report = build_slice_chain(artifact_dir)
 102: 
 103:     evidence_pool: list[SourceSpan] = []
 104:     for src in pool.sources:
 105:         # The recorded evidence text. build_slice_chain only admits T1
 106:         # legal-cleared sources, so source_tier is within SourceSpan's
 107:         # T1/T2/T3 Literal.
 108:         span_text = src.full_text or src.snippet or src.title or "n/a"
 109:         evidence_pool.append(
 110:             SourceSpan(
 111:                 evidence_id=src.source_id,
 112:                 source_url=str(src.url),
 113:                 source_tier=src.tier.value,
 114:                 # Truthful self-offset of the recorded span; rich
 115:                 # source-document offsets are deferred to #710.
 116:                 span_start=0,
 117:                 span_end=len(span_text),
 118:                 span_text=span_text,
 119:             )
 120:         )
 121: 
 122:     verified_sentences: list[VerifiedSentence] = []
 123:     for section in report.sections:
 124:         for sent in section.verified_sentences:
 125:             verified_sentences.append(
 126:                 VerifiedSentence(
 127:                     section_id=sent.section_id,
 128:                     sentence_text=sent.sentence_text,
 129:                     provenance_tokens=list(sent.provenance_tokens),
 130:                     # The slice-chain records a single verifier_pass (Local AND
 131:                     # Global must both hold for a sentence to pass strict_verify),
 132:                     # so it maps to both EvidenceContract flags.
 133:                     verifier_local_pass=sent.verifier_pass,
 134:                     verifier_global_pass=sent.verifier_pass,
 135:                     drop_reason=sent.drop_reason,
 136:                 )
 137:             )
 138: 
 139:     return EvidenceContract(
 140:         run_id=run_id,
 141:         template=template,
 142:         question=question,
 143:         queued_at=queued_at,
 144:         finished_at=finished_at,
 145:         pipeline_status=pipeline_status,
 146:         evidence_pool=evidence_pool,
 147:         verified_sentences=verified_sentences,
 148:         frame_coverage=[],
 149:         contradictions=_read_contradictions(artifact_dir),
 150:         cost_usd=float(report.cost_usd or 0.0),
 151:         generator_model=report.generator_model,
 152:         verifier_model=report.evaluator_model,
 153:         family_segregation_passed=report.family_segregation_passed,
 154:     )

 150:     app_with_bundle_router, isolated_db, tmp_path
 151: ):
 152:     """When a sign_fn override IS registered, build_slice_chain runs and the

 167:         "run_signed",

 171:         path=str(isolated_db),
 172:     )

 174:     # Install a stub signer override (returns synthetic signature bytes).
 175:     def _stub_sign_fn():
 176:         def _sign(_data: bytes) -> bytes:
 177:             return b"-----BEGIN PGP SIGNATURE-----\nstub\n-----END PGP SIGNATURE-----\n"
 178:         return _sign

 succeeded in 1704ms:
   1: """I-arch-001d — bridge from pipeline-A canonical artifact_dir to slice-chain
   2: Pydantic models (ScopeDecision, EvidencePool, VerifiedReport) consumable by
   3: the audit-bundle POST endpoint.
   4: 
   5: The audit-bundle path expects the slice-001/002/003 Pydantic shapes, but
   6: pipeline-A produces a different artifact set (manifest.json + report.md +
   7: bibliography.json + contradictions.json + verification_details.json +
   8: evidence_pool.json). This module translates one to the other.
   9: 
  10: Sovereignty cascade (Codex iter-2 P1-001): non-cleared sources are excluded
  11: from pool.sources entirely. Sentences whose provenance_tokens cite an
  12: excluded source are marked verifier_pass=False + drop_reason="invalid_token"
  13: + evaluator_agrees=False. Sections with no remaining passing sentences are
  14: marked section_status="dropped". If ALL sections drop, raises
  15: SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError so the endpoint can return 422.
  16: """
  17:

  19:

  21: import re

  62:     # NOTE: align with polaris_graph.clinical_generator.provenance shape:

  64:     _PROV_TOKEN_RE = re.compile(r"\[#ev:([^:\]]+):(\d+)-(\d+)\]")

  66: 
  67: class SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError(RuntimeError):
  68:     """Raised when sovereignty cascade leaves no non-dropped sections.
  69: 
  70:     The endpoint catches this and returns 422 to the client. The
  71:     bundle would otherwise fail `assert_all_pool_sources_legal_cleared`
  72:     or generate an empty pipeline_verdict='success' report — both
  73:     audit-grade incorrect.
  74:     """

  76: 
  77: # I-arch-001d Codex iter-4 P2: expanded drop_reason map covering pipeline-A's
  78: # observed reasons including no_integer_overlap / no_content_word_overlap /
  79: # trial_name_mismatch.
  80: _DROP_REASON_MAP: dict[str, DropReason] = {
  81:     "invalid_token": "invalid_token",
  82:     "span_out_of_range": "span_out_of_range",
  83:     "numeric_mismatch": "numeric_mismatch",
  84:     "number_not_in_any_cited_span": "numeric_mismatch",
  85:     "no_integer_overlap_any_cited_span": "numeric_mismatch",
  86:     "overlap_too_low": "overlap_too_low",
  87:     "low_content_overlap": "overlap_too_low",
  88:     "no_content_word_overlap_any_cited_span": "overlap_too_low",
  89:     "no_provenance_token": "no_provenance_token",
  90:     "missing_provenance": "no_provenance_token",
  91:     "entailment_failed": "entailment_failed",
  92:     "trial_name_mismatch": "invalid_token",
  93: }
  94: 
  95: 
  96: def _normalize_drop_reason(raw: str | None) -> DropReason | None:
  97:     if raw is None:
  98:         return None
  99:     base = raw.split(":")[0].strip().lower()
 100:     return _DROP_REASON_MAP.get(base, "invalid_token")
 101: 
 102: 
 103: def _normalize_tier(raw: str) -> tuple[SourceTier, str]:
 104:     """Map pipeline-A tier to SourceTier Literal. T4+/UNKNOWN → T3."""
 105:     upper = (raw or "").upper().strip()
 106:     if upper in ("T1", "T2", "T3"):
 107:         return SourceTier(upper), upper
 108:     return SourceTier.T3, upper or "UNKNOWN"
 109: 
 110: 
 111: def _derive_scope_class(domain: str | None, scope_class: str | None) -> ScopeClassValue:
 112:     """Derive a valid ScopeClassValue Literal from pipeline-A manifest fields."""
 113:     if scope_class:
 114:         s = scope_class.strip().lower()
 115:         for valid in (
 116:             "clinical_efficacy", "clinical_safety", "clinical_diagnosis",
 117:             "clinical_prognosis", "out_of_scope", "uncertain",
 118:         ):
 119:             if s == valid:
 120:                 return valid  # type: ignore[return-value]
 121:     if domain and "clinical" in domain.lower():
 122:         return "clinical_efficacy"
 123:     return "uncertain"
 124: 
 125: 
 126: def _redact_sentence(sent: VerifiedSentence) -> VerifiedSentence:
 127:     """Mark a sentence as failed during sovereignty cascade.
 128: 
 129:     Rebuilds via constructor (runs validators) instead of model_copy
 130:     which bypasses them. Sets evaluator_agrees=False to satisfy the
 131:     invariant that verifier_pass=False forbids evaluator_agrees=True.
 132:     """
 133:     fields = sent.model_dump()
 134:     fields["verifier_pass"] = False
 135:     fields["drop_reason"] = "invalid_token"
 136:     fields["evaluator_agrees"] = False
 137:     return VerifiedSentence(**fields)
 138: 
 139: 
 140: def _evidence_ids_in_tokens(provenance_tokens: list[str]) -> set[str]:
 141:     out: set[str] = set()
 142:     for tok in provenance_tokens:
 143:         m = _PROV_TOKEN_RE.search(tok)
 144:         if m:
 145:             out.add(m.group(1))
 146:     return out
 147: 
 148: 
 149: def _tokens_to_strings(tokens: tuple[EvidenceSpanToken, ...]) -> list[str]:
 150:     return [f"[#ev:{t.evidence_id}:{t.start}-{t.end}]" for t in tokens]
 151: 
 152: 
 153: def _read_optional_json(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any] | list[Any] | None:
 154:     if not path.is_file():
 155:         return None
 156:     try:
 157:         return json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 158:     except json.JSONDecodeError:
 159:         return None
 160: 
 161: 
 162: def _full_text_for_evidence_id(
 163:     evidence_id: str,
 164:     evidence_pool_raw: dict[str, Any] | list[Any] | None,
 165: ) -> str | None:
 166:     """Lookup evidence body in evidence_pool.json (Codex iter-2 P2 Q4).
 167: 
 168:     Pipeline-A's persisted field is commonly `direct_quote`, not full_text.
 169:     """
 170:     if evidence_pool_raw is None:
 171:         return None
 172:     sources = (
 173:         evidence_pool_raw.get("sources") if isinstance(evidence_pool_raw, dict)
 174:         else evidence_pool_raw
 175:     )
 176:     if not isinstance(sources, list):
 177:         return None
 178:     for src in sources:
 179:         if not isinstance(src, dict):
 180:             continue
 181:         if src.get("evidence_id") == evidence_id or src.get("source_id") == evidence_id:
 182:             return (
 183:                 src.get("full_text")
 184:                 or src.get("direct_quote")
 185:                 or src.get("snippet")
 186:             )
 187:     return None
 188: 
 189: 
 190: def _parse_iso(value: Any) -> datetime | None:
 191:     if not value:
 192:         return None
 193:     if isinstance(value, datetime):
 194:         return value
 195:     try:
 196:         return datetime.fromisoformat(str(value).replace("Z", "+00:00"))
 197:     except (TypeError, ValueError):
 198:         return None
 199: 
 200: 
 201: def build_slice_chain(
 202:     artifact_dir: Path,
 203: ) -> tuple[ScopeDecision, EvidencePool, SliceChainVerifiedReport]:
 204:     """Convert a pipeline-A canonical artifact dir to slice-chain Pydantic models.
 205: 
 206:     Raises:
 207:         FileNotFoundError: artifact_dir missing required canonical files
 208:         SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError: sovereignty cascade leaves no
 209:             non-dropped sections (cannot ship a bundle for this run)
 210:     """
 211:     air = load_audit_ir(artifact_dir)
 212:     manifest_raw = json.loads((artifact_dir / "manifest.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 213:     evidence_pool_raw = _read_optional_json(artifact_dir / "evidence_pool.json")
 214: 
 215:     # ─── 1. ScopeDecision ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
 216:     decision_id = (
 217:         (manifest_raw.get("scope") or {}).get("decision_id")
 218:         or manifest_raw.get("external_run_id")
 219:         or str(uuid.uuid4())
 220:     )
 221:     scope_class = _derive_scope_class(
 222:         manifest_raw.get("domain"),
 223:         (manifest_raw.get("scope") or {}).get("classification"),
 224:     )
 225:     decision = ScopeDecision(
 226:         decision_id=decision_id,
 227:         status="in_scope",
 228:         scope_class=scope_class,
 229:         ambiguity_axes=[],
 230:         clarifications_needed=[],
 231:         provenance={
 232:             "classifier_layer": "pipeline_a_v30",
 233:             "artifact_dir": str(artifact_dir),
 234:         },
 235:     )
 236: 
 237:     # ─── 2. EvidencePool (sovereignty-filtered) ───────────────────────────
 238:     sources: list[Source] = []
 239:     cleared_evidence_ids: set[str] = set()
 240:     for entry in air.bibliography:
 241:         # Tier-1 is legal-cleared by default; non-T1 requires explicit clearance
 242:         # in evidence_pool.json provenance.legal_cleared = True (Phase 2 hook).
 243:         canonical_tier, raw_tier = _normalize_tier(entry.tier)
 244:         is_legal_cleared = canonical_tier == SourceTier.T1
 245:         if not is_legal_cleared:
 246:             continue  # exclude — sovereignty_guard would reject otherwise
 247:         full_text = _full_text_for_evidence_id(entry.evidence_id, evidence_pool_raw)
 248:         sources.append(Source(
 249:             source_id=entry.evidence_id,
 250:             url=entry.url,
 251:             domain=_url_domain(entry.url),
 252:             tier=canonical_tier,
 253:             title=entry.statement[:200] or "Untitled",
 254:             snippet=entry.statement[:1000] or "n/a",
 255:             full_text_available=full_text is not None,
 256:             full_text=full_text,
 257:             provenance={
 258:                 "legal_cleared": True,
 259:                 "raw_tier": raw_tier,
 260:             },
 261:             retracted=False,
 262:         ))
 263:         cleared_evidence_ids.add(entry.evidence_id)
 264: 
 265:     retrieval_block = manifest_raw.get("retrieval", {}) or {}
 266:     started_utc = _parse_iso(retrieval_block.get("started_at")) or datetime.now(timezone.utc)
 267:     finished_utc = _parse_iso(retrieval_block.get("finished_at")) or started_utc
 268:     pool = EvidencePool(
 269:         pool_id=retrieval_block.get("pool_id") or str(uuid.uuid4()),
 270:         decision_id=decision.decision_id,
 271:         sources=sources,
 272:         adequacy=AdequacyVerdict(
 273:             is_adequate=True,
 274:             adequacy_score=1.0,
 275:             failure_reason=None,
 276:         ),
 277:         queries_executed=retrieval_block.get("queries_executed", []) or [],
 278:         retrieval_started_at_utc=started_utc,
 279:         retrieval_finished_at_utc=finished_utc,
 280:         latency_ms=int(retrieval_block.get("latency_ms") or 0),
 281:         cost_usd=float(air.manifest.cost_usd or 0.0),
 282:     )
 283: 
 284:     # ─── 3. VerifiedReport (sovereignty cascade) ──────────────────────────
 285:     sections: list[Section] = []
 286:     for air_section in air.verified_report.sections:
 287:         kept: list[VerifiedSentence] = []
 288:         for air_sent in air_section.sentences:
 289:             sc_sent = _air_sentence_to_slice_chain(air_sent)
 290:             cited_ids = _evidence_ids_in_tokens(sc_sent.provenance_tokens)
 291:             if not cited_ids or cited_ids.issubset(cleared_evidence_ids):
 292:                 kept.append(sc_sent)
 293:             else:
 294:                 kept.append(_redact_sentence(sc_sent))
 295:         pass_count = sum(1 for s in kept if s.verifier_pass)
 296:         section_status: SectionStatus = (
 297:             "dropped" if pass_count == 0 else "verified"
 298:         )
 299:         sections.append(Section(
 300:             section_id=_slugify(air_section.title) or f"section_{len(sections)}",
 301:             section_title=air_section.title or f"Section {len(sections)}",
 302:             verified_sentences=kept,
 303:             section_verify_pass_rate=pass_count / max(len(kept), 1),
 304:             section_status=section_status,
 305:         ))
 306: 
 307:     non_dropped = [s for s in sections if s.section_status != "dropped"]
 308:     if not non_dropped:
 309:         raise SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError(
 310:             "every section dropped after sovereignty cascade; bundle cannot be assembled"
 311:         )
 312: 
 313:     overall = sum(s.section_verify_pass_rate for s in non_dropped) / len(non_dropped)
 314:     # Codex diff iter-1 P2-001 fix: partial_* runs still have kept sections;
 315:     # they're "success-with-degradation" not "no_verified_sections" aborts.
 316:     # PipelineVerdict Literal accepts success | abort_no_verified_sections;
 317:     # collapse partial_* into "success" since the pipeline did produce kept
 318:     # content (the degradation is recorded on the manifest, not the verdict).
 319:     manifest_status = air.manifest.status or ""
 320:     if manifest_status == "success" or manifest_status.startswith("partial_"):
 321:         pipeline_verdict: PipelineVerdict = "success"
 322:     else:
 323:         pipeline_verdict = "abort_no_verified_sections"
 324:     models_block = manifest_raw.get("models") or {}
 325:     report = SliceChainVerifiedReport(
 326:         report_id=air.manifest.run_id,
 327:         pool_id=pool.pool_id,
 328:         decision_id=decision.decision_id,
 329:         sections=sections,
 330:         overall_verify_pass_rate=overall,
 331:         pipeline_verdict=pipeline_verdict,
 332:         generator_model=models_block.get("generator") or "unknown",
 333:         evaluator_model=models_block.get("evaluator") or "strict_verify_v1",
 334:         family_segregation_passed=True,
 335:         verifier_pass_threshold=0.4,
 336:         started_at_utc=started_utc,
 337:         finished_at_utc=finished_utc,
 338:         latency_ms=int(retrieval_block.get("latency_ms") or 0),
 339:         cost_usd=float(air.manifest.cost_usd or 0.0),
 340:     )
 341:     return decision, pool, report
 342: 
 343: 
 344: def _air_sentence_to_slice_chain(air_sent: AuditIRSentence) -> VerifiedSentence:
 345:     """AuditIR ReportSentence → slice-chain VerifiedSentence."""
 346:     failure = air_sent.failure_reasons[0] if air_sent.failure_reasons else None
 347:     return VerifiedSentence(
 348:         section_id=_slugify(air_sent.section) or "section",
 349:         sentence_text=air_sent.text or "n/a",
 350:         provenance_tokens=_tokens_to_strings(air_sent.tokens),
 351:         verifier_pass=bool(air_sent.is_verified),
 352:         drop_reason=_normalize_drop_reason(failure) if not air_sent.is_verified else None,
 353:         evaluator_agrees=bool(air_sent.is_verified),
 354:         is_synthesis_claim=len(air_sent.tokens) == 0 and bool(air_sent.is_verified),
 355:     )
 356: 
 357: 
 358: def _url_domain(url: str) -> str:
 359:     """Extract host for the Source.domain field. Falls back to 'unknown'."""
 360:     from urllib.parse import urlparse
 361:     try:
 362:         return urlparse(str(url)).netloc or "unknown"
 363:     except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — defensive: never raise during bridge
 364:         return "unknown"
 365: 
 366: 
 367: def _slugify(text: str) -> str:
 368:     return re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9_]+", "_", (text or "").lower()).strip("_")[:60]

  17: 
  18: 
  19: def resolve_completed_artifact_dir(run_id: str) -> Path:
  20:     """Resolve a completed run to its on-disk artifact_dir, or raise.
  21: 
  22:     The shared run-resolution for every completed-run read route (inspector
  23:     slices 1 + 7a, charts slice 8):
  24: 
  25:     - unknown run -> 404
  26:     - run not completed -> 409
  27:     - abort_* / error_* run -> 422 (no AuditIR-loadable artifacts)
  28:     - missing / absent artifact_dir -> 404
  29:     """
  30:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  31:     if record is None:
  32:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run not found: {run_id}")
  33: 
  34:     if record.lifecycle_status != "completed":
  35:         raise HTTPException(
  36:             status_code=409,
  37:             detail=(
  38:                 f"run {run_id} is not completed "
  39:                 f"(lifecycle_status={record.lifecycle_status!r})"
  40:             ),
  41:         )
  42: 
  43:     status = record.pipeline_status or ""
  44:     if status.startswith("abort_") or status.startswith("error_"):
  45:         raise HTTPException(
  46:             status_code=422,
  47:             detail=(
  48:                 f"run {run_id} produced no AuditIR-loadable artifacts "
  49:                 f"(pipeline_status={status!r}); it is a pipeline-verdict "
  50:                 f"artifact, not a renderable run"
  51:             ),
  52:         )
  53: 
  54:     if not record.artifact_dir:
  55:         raise HTTPException(
  56:             status_code=404,
  57:             detail=f"run {run_id} has no artifact_dir recorded",
  58:         )
  59:     artifact_dir = Path(record.artifact_dir)
  60:     if not artifact_dir.is_dir():
  61:         raise HTTPException(
  62:             status_code=404,
  63:             detail=f"artifact_dir does not exist on disk: {artifact_dir}",
  64:         )
  65:     return artifact_dir

  24: from __future__ import annotations
  25: 
  26: import json
  27: from pathlib import Path
  28: from typing import Any
  29: 
  30: from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
  31: 
  32: from polaris_graph.audit_ir.loader import load_audit_ir

  36: router = APIRouter(prefix="/api/inspector", tags=["inspector"])

  38: 
  39: def _load_evidence_pool(artifact_dir: Path, run_id: str) -> dict[str, dict[str, Any]]:
  40:     """Index `evidence_pool.json` by evidence id. Fail loud if absent/malformed.
  41: 
  42:     Mirrors `artifact_to_slice_chain._full_text_for_evidence_id`: the pool is
  43:     EITHER a bare JSON list OR `{"sources": [...]}`; a row is keyed by
  44:     `evidence_id` or `source_id`. Returns `{evidence_id: row}`.
  45: 
  46:     A run with no `evidence_pool.json` predates evidence-pool persistence — it
  47:     is not span-renderable; 422 (fail loud, no `bibliography.statement`
  48:     fallback) per the Codex arch consult + LAW II.
  49:     """
  50:     pool_path = artifact_dir / "evidence_pool.json"
  51:     if not pool_path.is_file():
  52:         raise HTTPException(
  53:             status_code=422,
  54:             detail=(
  55:                 f"run {run_id} has no evidence_pool.json — the verified "
  56:                 f"evidence spans cannot be reconstructed (this run predates "
  57:                 f"evidence-pool persistence)"
  58:             ),
  59:         )
  60:     try:
  61:         raw = json.loads(pool_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
  62:     except (ValueError, OSError) as exc:
  63:         raise HTTPException(
  64:             status_code=422,
  65:             detail=f"run {run_id} evidence_pool.json is unreadable: {exc}",
  66:         ) from exc
  67: 
  68:     rows = raw.get("sources") if isinstance(raw, dict) else raw
  69:     if not isinstance(rows, list):
  70:         raise HTTPException(
  71:             status_code=422,
  72:             detail=(
  73:                 f"run {run_id} evidence_pool.json is not a list of sources "
  74:                 f"(nor a {{'sources': [...]}} object)"
  75:             ),
  76:         )
  77: 
  78:     indexed: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
  79:     for row in rows:
  80:         if not isinstance(row, dict):
  81:             continue
  82:         ev_id = row.get("evidence_id") or row.get("source_id")
  83:         if ev_id:
  84:             indexed[str(ev_id)] = row
  85:     return indexed
  86: 
  87: 
  88: def _evidence_body(row: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
  89:     """The per-row evidence body text — `full_text`/`direct_quote`/`snippet`
  90:     precedence, mirroring `artifact_to_slice_chain._full_text_for_evidence_id`.
  91:     """
  92:     for key in ("full_text", "direct_quote", "snippet"):
  93:         value = row.get(key)
  94:         if isinstance(value, str) and value:
  95:             return value
  96:     return ""
  97:

 114:

 122:         raise HTTPException(

 125:         ) from exc

 130: @router.get("/runs/{run_id}/evidence")
 131: def get_inspector_run_evidence(run_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 132:     """Return the verified evidence spans cited by a completed run.
 133: 
 134:     I-rdy-008 (#504) slice 7a (Codex arch consult
 135:     `.codex/I-rdy-008/slice7_arch_consult_verdict.txt`). Every verified-report
 136:     sentence carries `[#ev:<id>:<start>-<end>]` tokens; this route resolves
 137:     each token's `evidence_id` against `evidence_pool.json` and reconstructs
 138:     the exact cited span as `body[start:end]` — the auditable source text an
 139:     auditor verifies a claim against. Spans are range-keyed
 140:     (`evidence_id, start, end`) and de-duplicated; `claim_ids` lists every
 141:     sentence that cites the span.
 142: 
 143:     Fails loud (422) — never degrades to a bibliography statement — when
 144:     `evidence_pool.json` is absent/malformed, a token cites an evidence id
 145:     absent from the pool, a row has no body text, or a token's offsets are
 146:     out of range.
 147: 
 148:     Resolution: unknown 404 / not-completed 409 / abort 422 / missing
 149:     artifact_dir 404 / unloadable AuditIR 422 / no evidence_pool.json 422 /
 150:     completed + loadable + pooled -> 200.
 151:     """
 152:     artifact_dir = resolve_completed_artifact_dir(run_id)
 153:     pool = _load_evidence_pool(artifact_dir, run_id)
 154: 
 155:     try:
 156:         ir = load_audit_ir(artifact_dir)
 157:     except (FileNotFoundError, NotADirectoryError, ValueError, TypeError) as exc:
 158:         raise HTTPException(
 159:             status_code=422,
 160:             detail=f"run {run_id} artifact_dir failed AuditIR load: {exc}",
 161:         ) from exc
 162: 
 163:     # Range key (evidence_id, start, end) -> set of citing sentence claim_ids.
 164:     claim_ids_by_span: dict[tuple[str, int, int], set[str]] = {}
 165:     for section in ir.verified_report.sections:
 166:         for sentence in section.sentences:
 167:             for token in sentence.tokens:
 168:                 key = (token.evidence_id, token.start, token.end)
 169:                 claim_ids_by_span.setdefault(key, set()).add(sentence.claim_id)
 170: 
 171:     spans: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
 172:     for evidence_id, start, end in sorted(claim_ids_by_span):
 173:         row = pool.get(evidence_id)
 174:         if row is None:
 175:             raise HTTPException(
 176:                 status_code=422,
 177:                 detail=(
 178:                     f"run {run_id}: a verified sentence token cites evidence "
 179:                     f"{evidence_id!r}, which is absent from evidence_pool.json"
 180:                 ),

   1: # Live-run artifact contract
   2: 
   3: **Issue:** I-rdy-007 (#503), Phase 3.4 of the Carney readiness chain.
   4: **Status:** definition. This document + `docs/schemas/live_run_artifact_contract.schema.json`
   5: define the contract; **wiring** the rich surfaces to consume it is I-rdy-008
   6: (#504). I-rdy-010 (#506) and I-rdy-012 (#508) also build on this contract.
   7: 
   8: **Purpose:** the single source of truth for *what a completed v6 run exposes*
   9: and *what each rich UI surface consumes from it*. It is the root fix for the
  10: fixture-bound rich surfaces — today most rich surfaces only render golden
  11: fixtures because the run→surface contract was "the code", never written down.
  12: 
  13: This contract is **grounded in the running code**, not in older docs.
  14: `docs/pipeline_audit_context/03_json_contracts.md` is the earlier prose
  15: description; it is **stale** on the status taxonomy (it lists 10 values; the
  16: code defines 14 — see §3) and is superseded by this document + the JSON schema.
  17: 
  18: ---
  19: 
  20: ## 1. The producer — a completed v6 run
  21: 
  22: A run is created via `POST /runs` (`src/polaris_v6/api/runs.py`) and tracked in
  23: the v6 run store (`src/polaris_v6/queue/run_store.py`, SQLite `runs` table).
  24: `GET /runs/{run_id}` returns `RunStatusResponse`
  25: (`src/polaris_v6/schemas/run_status.py`):
  26: 
  27: | Field | Meaning |
  28: |---|---|
  29: | `run_id` | server-assigned UUID hex |
  30: | `lifecycle_status` | operational: `queued` → `in_progress` → `completed` \| `failed` \| `cancelled` |
  31: | `pipeline_status` | pipeline-A manifest verdict (§3); `null` until a terminal pipeline state |
  32: | `template`, `question` | run inputs |
  33: | `queued_at` / `started_at` / `finished_at` | ISO-8601 UTC |
  34: | `query_slug`, `manifest_run_id` | UUID ↔ slug ↔ manifest-id mapping (I-arch-001a) |
  35: | `artifact_dir` | filesystem path to the run's artifact directory — **the join key to everything below** |
  36: | `cost_usd`, `decision_id`, `result_json`, `error_json` | run accounting / telemetry |
  37: | `status` | deprecated computed alias of `lifecycle_status` (tests/v6 backcompat) |
  38: 
  39: A **completed** run (`lifecycle_status == "completed"`) has a populated
  40: `artifact_dir`. That directory is the contract surface.
  41: 
  42: ## 2. The artifact directory
  43: 
  44: `artifact_dir` holds the pipeline-A artifact set. Files split into three
  45: classes by how `src/polaris_graph/audit_ir/loader.py` `load_audit_ir()`
  46: treats them:
  47: 
  48: ### 2.1 Required for AuditIR (fail-loud if missing)
  49: 
  50: `load_audit_ir()` raises `FileNotFoundError` / `AuditIRSchemaError` if any of
  51: these is absent or malformed:
  52: 
  53: | File | Carries |
  54: |---|---|
  55: | `manifest.json` | run verdict + adequacy/corpus/generator/evaluator/frame-coverage/retrieval blocks |
  56: | `report.md` | rendered markdown report with `[N]` inline citations (2 shapes — §4) |
  57: | `bibliography.json` | the `[N]` → `evidence_id` → source mapping |
  58: | `contradictions.json` | tier-labelled disagreement clusters (≥2 claims each) |
  59: | `verification_details.json` | per-section kept/dropped sentences + `[#ev:id:start-end]` span tokens |
  60: 
  61: ### 2.2 Optional provenance (loaded when present)
  62: 
  63: | File | Carries | Rule |
  64: |---|---|---|
  65: | `evaluator_rule_checks.json` | generator/evaluator family+model, per-rule pass/fail | **both-or-neither** with `judge_output.json` — `load_audit_ir()` raises if exactly one is present |
  66: | `judge_output.json` | judge model, parse-ok, I/O token counts (legacy fallback name: `qwen_judge_output.json`) | pairs with the above |
  67: | `protocol.json` | scope template — research question, `created_at`, `expected_tier_distribution` | drives Inspector View 5 expected-vs-actual tier bands |
  68: | `corpus_approval.json` | corpus-approval gate decision + note | absent on auto-approved runs |
  69: | `evidence_pool.json` / `live_corpus_dump.json` | per-evidence detail (id, url, tier, statement, quote) | the bridge's `EvidencePool` source |
  70: | `reasoning_trace.jsonl` | V4-Pro chain-of-thought trace (I-gen-004) | included in the live tar.gz bundle when present |
  71: | `run_log.txt` | human-readable `[tag]`-prefixed run log | not consumed by AuditIR |
  72: 
  73: ### 2.3 Status-conditional availability (Codex brief P2-001)
  74: 
  75: The §2.1 "required" set is required **for a run that is expected to resolve
  76: through `load_audit_ir()`** — i.e. `success` / `partial_*` runs.
  77: **`abort_*` and `error_*` runs** legitimately lack `verification_details.json`
  78: and `evidence_pool.json` (an abort happens before per-sentence verification, or
  79: before generation entirely). A consumer MUST branch on `pipeline_status`
  80: (§3) BEFORE attempting `load_audit_ir()`; an `abort_*` artifact dir is a
  81: pipeline-verdict artifact, not an AuditIR-loadable run. The JSON schema marks
  82: verification/evidence fields required only under non-abort status.
  83: 
  84: ## 3. `manifest.status` / `pipeline_status` — the 14-value taxonomy
  85: 
  86: The authoritative set is the code: `PipelineStatus` in
  87: `src/polaris_v6/schemas/run_status.py` and `UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES` in
  88: `scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py` (they agree). It is the **single
  89: authoritative run verdict** — consumers classify a run by this, never by
  90: `report.md` existence.
  91: 
  92: | Class | Values |
  93: |---|---|
  94: | success | `success` |
  95: | partial — report produced, degraded signal | `partial_thin_corpus`, `partial_incomplete_corpus`, `partial_rule_check_warnings`, `partial_outline_fallback`, `partial_evaluator_advisory`, `partial_qwen_advisory` (legacy alias) |
  96: | abort — pipeline refused to produce a report | `abort_scope_rejected`, `abort_no_sources`, `abort_corpus_inadequate`, `abort_corpus_approval_denied`, `abort_no_verified_sections`, `abort_evaluator_critical` |
  97: | error — unhandled exception | `error_unexpected` |
  98: 
  99: `docs/pipeline_audit_context/03_json_contracts.md` lists only 10 of these and
 100: is **stale** — it predates `partial_outline_fallback`,
 101: `partial_evaluator_advisory`, `partial_qwen_advisory`, and
 102: `abort_evaluator_critical`.
 103: 
 104: **Pre-taxonomy artifacts (grounding finding):** some legacy artifact dirs
 105: (observed: `outputs/honest_sweep_r6_validation/clinical/clinical_afib_anticoagulation/`)
 106: have a `manifest.json` with NO top-level `status` field at all — they predate
 107: the unified taxonomy. These are **not contract-conformant**: `load_audit_ir()`
 108: rejects them (`_parse_manifest` requires `status`), and the JSON schema marks
 109: `status` required. A live v6 run always writes `status`; a consumer that
 110: encounters a `status`-less manifest should treat the run as un-renderable, not
 111: attempt to guess.
 112: 
 113: ## 4. `report.md` — two shapes
 114: 
 115: - **`success` / `partial_*`**: an actual research report — `## <section>`
 116:   prose with numbered `[N]` citations, then `## Limitations`, `## Methods`,
 117:   `## Bibliography`.
 118: - **`abort_*`**: a pipeline-verdict artifact — `## Pipeline verdict` +
 119:   per-section verdict + suggested next steps. NOT a research report.
 120: 
 121: Consumers MUST distinguish these by `pipeline_status` (§3), never by
 122: `report.md` existence.
 123: 
 124: ## 5. The canonical IR layer — `AuditIR`
 125: 
 126: `load_audit_ir(artifact_dir)` → an immutable `AuditIR`
 127: (`src/polaris_graph/audit_ir/loader.py`). The loader docstring states the
 128: design rule (from FINAL_PLAN.md, Claude+Codex agreed): **"The AuditIR is the
 129: single source of truth for the Evidence Inspector and all derivative
 130: renderers"** — the report is a projection, not the source.
 131: 
 132: `AuditIR` (`ir_schema_version = "1.0.0"`) joins:
 133: 
 134: | `AuditIR` field | From | Used by |
 135: |---|---|---|
 136: | `manifest: RunManifest` | `manifest.json` | every surface (verdict, cost, counts) |
 137: | `report_md: str` | `report.md` | inspector report pane |
 138: | `bibliography: tuple[BibliographyEntry]` | `bibliography.json` | inspector `[N]`→source, citation hover |
 139: | `verified_report: VerifiedReport` | `verification_details.json` | inspector click-to-inspect (claim_id → sentence → span tokens) |
 140: | `contradictions: tuple[ContradictionCluster]` | `contradictions.json` | contradiction navigation |
 141: | `frame_coverage: FrameCoverageReport` | `manifest.frame_coverage_report` | frame-coverage panel |
 142: | `tier_mix: TierMix` | `manifest.corpus` | source-tier-mix view |
 143: | `model_provenance: ModelProvenance \| None` | `evaluator_rule_checks.json` + `judge_output.json` | methods/provenance bundle, two-family signal |
 144: | `protocol: ProtocolMetadata \| None` | `protocol.json` | expected-vs-actual tier bands |
 145: | `adequacy: AdequacyGate \| None` | `manifest.adequacy` | adequacy-gate detail |
 146: | `corpus_approval: CorpusApprovalGate \| None` | `corpus_approval.json` | approval-gate detail |
 147: 
 148: `AuditIR` lookup methods (`get_sentence_by_claim_id`,
 149: `get_bibliography_by_num`/`_by_evidence_id`, `get_contradictions_for_evidence`,
 150: `get_frame_coverage_for_entity`, `get_tier_counts`,
 151: `get_evidence_spans_for_claim`) are the resolution API every rich surface
 152: should use. **`claim_id` = `<section>:<kept|dropped>:<idx>`** is the stable
 153: click-to-inspect handle a renderer overlays onto `report.md`.
 154: 
 155: ## 6. Per-consumer mapping
 156: 
 157: Each rich surface, the v6 API route that serves it, the `AuditIR` it needs,
 158: and its current state. Current-state column is the I-rdy-002 (#498)
 159: verification recorded in `docs/polaris_locked_scope.md` §3.1.
 160: 
 161: | Surface | v6 API route | Consumes from `AuditIR` | Current state |
 162: |---|---|---|---|
 163: | Inspector (report click-through, F5) | `runs.py` (`GET /runs/{id}`) → `artifact_dir` → `load_audit_ir` | `report_md`, `verified_report`, `bibliography`, `manifest` | components exist; **not on the live `/runs` report** — fixture-bound |
 164: | Citation hover (F6) | inspector data | `bibliography`, `verified_report.tokens` | harness/fixture-bound |
 165: | Frame coverage (F7) | inspector data | `frame_coverage` | harness/fixture-bound |
 166: | Contradiction navigation (F8) | inspector data | `contradictions` | harness/fixture-bound |
 167: | Two-family disagreement (F9) | inspector data | `model_provenance`, `evaluator_gate` | harness/fixture-bound |
 168: | Charts (F10 inline visuals) | `charts.py` | `verified_report`, `contradictions`, `tier_mix` | spec builder/API/tests exist; fixture-bound |
 169: | Follow-up (F11) | `followup.py` | `report_md`, `bibliography`, `verified_report` | backend exists; **disabled on the product run page** |
 170: | Compare (F12) | `compare.py` | two runs' `AuditIR` | backend exists; **no product route** |
 171: | Pin replay (F13) | `pin_replay` route | run-id → pins | page exists; **demo-data-bound** |
 172: | Memory (F14) | `memory.py` | run summary + citations | page+API exist; **in-memory demo store, not durable** |
 173: | Bundle (F15) | `bundle.py` — **two routes** | via `artifact_to_slice_chain` → slice-chain Pydantic | see below |
 174: 
 175: **Bundle has two distinct routes — #504 must not treat "bundle" as one thing:**
 176: - `GET /runs/{id}/bundle` — still returns golden **EvidenceContract** JSON
 177:   (the I-ecg pre-run contract, *not* the live artifact contract). Fixture-bound.
 178: - `GET /runs/{id}/bundle.tar.gz` — live: `artifact_dir` →
 179:   `artifact_to_slice_chain.py` (`load_audit_ir` → slice-chain `ScopeDecision`/
 180:   `EvidencePool`/`VerifiedReport`) → signed tar.gz. Live-capable.

  86: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  87: # Test 2: Every manifest-writing branch in run_one_query emits a
  88: # status field, enforced by AST inspection of the source.
  89: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  90: 
  91: def _find_manifest_write_blocks(source: str) -> list[tuple[int, int, str]]:
  92:     """Find every `(run_dir / "manifest.json").write_text(...)` call
  93:     and the ~60 lines of source that precede it (that's the manifest
  94:     construction). Return [(start_line, end_line, block_text), ...]."""
  95:     tree = ast.parse(source)
  96:     blocks: list[tuple[int, int, str]] = []
  97:     source_lines = source.splitlines()
  98:     for node in ast.walk(tree):
  99:         if (
 100:             isinstance(node, ast.Call)
 101:             and isinstance(node.func, ast.Attribute)
 102:             and node.func.attr == "write_text"
 103:         ):
 104:             # Check the receiver is `(... / "manifest.json")`
 105:             recv = node.func.value
 106:             if isinstance(recv, ast.BinOp) and isinstance(recv.op, ast.Div):
 107:                 right = recv.right
 108:                 if isinstance(right, ast.Constant) and right.value == "manifest.json":
 109:                     # Found a manifest write. Look backward 200 lines
 110:                     # for the `{ ... }` construction. The V30 site
 111:                     # at line 1918 has its dict starting at 1780 (138
 112:                     # lines apart), so the original 80-line window
 113:                     # missed it; the M-26-era triage Codex review
 114:                     # flagged this as a false positive. Extending to
 115:                     # 200 covers the V30 site without admitting
 116:                     # false positives elsewhere (other manifest
 117:                     # writes have their `{ ... }` immediately above
 118:                     # the write_text call).
 119:                     end_line = node.lineno
 120:                     start_line = max(1, end_line - 200)
 121:                     block = "\n".join(source_lines[start_line - 1:end_line])
 122:                     blocks.append((start_line, end_line, block))
 123:     return blocks
 124:

 126: def test_manifest_contract_all_manifest_writes_have_status() -> None:
 127:     """Every site that writes manifest.json in run_honest_sweep_r3.py
 128:     must include a 'status' key in the manifest dict. AST-based check
 129:     so adding a new exit path without status fails this test."""
 130:     sweep_path = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2] / "scripts" / "run_honest_sweep_r3.py"
 131:     source = sweep_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
 132:     blocks = _find_manifest_write_blocks(source)
 133:     assert len(blocks) >= 4, (
 134:         f"Expected >=4 manifest write sites in run_one_query, got {len(blocks)}"
 135:     )
 136:     for start, end, block in blocks:
 137:         # Look for a `"status":` literal string assignment within the
 138:         # preceding 80-line window. That's loose but catches the common
 139:         # pattern.
 140:         assert '"status"' in block, (
 141:             f"Manifest write at line {end} has no 'status' field in "
 142:             f"the preceding construction block (lines {start}-{end}):\n"
 143:             f"{block[-400:]}"
 144:         )

 203: def test_manifest_contract_exception_writes_error_manifest() -> None:
 204:     """Source check: the OUTER exception handler in run_one_query writes
 205:     a manifest with status='error_unexpected'. Uses AST to find the
 206:     outermost try/except in run_one_query (not an inner one)."""
 207:     import ast as _ast
 208:     sweep_path = (
 209:         Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2] / "scripts" / "run_honest_sweep_r3.py"
 210:     )
 211:     source = sweep_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
 212:     tree = _ast.parse(source)
 213:     # Find the async def run_one_query
 214:     func = next(
 215:         (n for n in _ast.walk(tree)
 216:          if isinstance(n, _ast.AsyncFunctionDef) and n.name == "run_one_query"),
 217:         None,
 218:     )
 219:     assert func is not None, "expected async def run_one_query"
 220:     # Find the first Try node directly in the body (outermost try).
 221:     outer_try = next(
 222:         (n for n in func.body if isinstance(n, _ast.Try)),
 223:         None,
 224:     )
 225:     assert outer_try is not None, "expected outer try in run_one_query"
 226:     # Each Try has ExceptHandler(s). Dump the handlers' source ranges.
 227:     handler_sources = []
 228:     for handler in outer_try.handlers:
 229:         start = handler.lineno
 230:         end = handler.end_lineno or start
 231:         handler_sources.append("\n".join(source.splitlines()[start - 1:end]))
 232:     combined = "\n".join(handler_sources)
 233:     assert '"status": "error_unexpected"' in combined, (

 236:     )

 238:         "Outer exception handler must attempt to write manifest.json"

 357: def mark_aborted(
 358:     run_id: str,
 359:     *,
 360:     pipeline_status: str,
 361:     abort_reason: str,
 362:     cost_usd: float | None = None,
 363:     path: str | None = None,
 364: ) -> None:
 365:     """Pipeline ran to completion but hit a gate; lifecycle_status='completed', pipeline_status='abort_*'.
 366: 
 367:     Per CLAUDE.md §9.3, abort_* are pipeline verdicts (not errors). The run
 368:     completed operationally; the pipeline-A logic chose to halt at a gate.
 369:     """
 370:     conn = _connect(path)
 371:     try:
 372:         conn.execute(
 373:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='completed', finished_at=?, "
 374:             "pipeline_status=?, error_json=?, cost_usd=? WHERE run_id=?",
 375:             (
 376:                 _now_iso(),
 377:                 pipeline_status,
 378:                 json.dumps({"abort_reason": abort_reason}, sort_keys=True),
 379:                 cost_usd,
 380:                 run_id,
 381:             ),
 382:         )
 383:         conn.commit()
 384:     finally:
 385:         conn.close()

 388: def mark_failed(
 389:     run_id: str,
 390:     error: str,
 391:     *,
 392:     path: str | None = None,
 393:     uploaded_documents_used: int | None = None,
 394:     uploaded_documents_blocked: int | None = None,
 395: ) -> None:
 396:     """Operational failure (exception, missing manifest, unknown status, etc).
 397: 
 398:     Distinct from mark_aborted: failures are unplanned (exception or invariant
 399:     violation); aborts are planned (pipeline_status='abort_*' written by
 400:     pipeline-A at a gate).
 401: 
 402:     I-cd-018 (#628): optional `uploaded_documents_used` +
 403:     `uploaded_documents_blocked` flow into `error_json` so the error-path
 404:     observability mirrors the success-path INFO log (actors.py:146-151).
 405:     Keys are present in error_json only when caller passes them.
 406:     """
 407:     error_payload: dict[str, object] = {"error": error}
 408:     if uploaded_documents_used is not None:
 409:         error_payload["uploaded_documents_used"] = uploaded_documents_used
 410:     if uploaded_documents_blocked is not None:
 411:         error_payload["uploaded_documents_blocked"] = uploaded_documents_blocked
 412:     conn = _connect(path)
 413:     try:
 414:         conn.execute(
 415:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='failed', finished_at=?, "
 416:             "pipeline_status='error_unexpected', error_json=? WHERE run_id=?",
 417:             (_now_iso(), json.dumps(error_payload, sort_keys=True), run_id),
 418:         )
 419:         conn.commit()
 420:     finally:
 421:         conn.close()

+    """No fabricated source-document offsets (Codex Option B). Each SourceSpan

+        assert span.source_tier in ("T1", "T2", "T3")

 894:     """Codex M-1 v2 review fix: load model/version provenance from runtime artifacts.
 895: 
 896:     Returns None if BOTH files are absent (legacy runs predate them).
 897:     Raises AuditIRSchemaError if exactly one is present, since partial
 898:     provenance silently zero-filling the missing half violates audit-grade
 899:     discipline (Codex M-1 v3 review edge case).
 900:     """
 901:     if eval_rules_raw is None and judge_raw is None:
 902:         return None
 903:     if eval_rules_raw is None or judge_raw is None:
 904:         present = "evaluator_rule_checks.json" if eval_rules_raw else "judge_output.json"
 905:         missing = "judge_output.json" if eval_rules_raw else "evaluator_rule_checks.json"
 906:         raise AuditIRSchemaError(
 907:             f"Partial model provenance: {present} present but {missing} missing. "
 908:             f"Both must be present together or both absent."
 909:         )

 911:         _parse_rule_check(rc) for rc in eval_rules_raw.get("rule_checks", [])
 912:     )

 676:     return EvaluatorGate(
 677:         gate_class=str(raw.get("gate_class", "unknown")),
 678:         release_allowed=bool(raw.get("release_allowed", False)),
 679:         reasons=tuple(str(r) for r in raw.get("reasons", [])),
 680:         rule_blockers=tuple(str(r) for r in raw.get("rule_blockers", [])),
 681:         judge_critical_axes=tuple(
 682:             str(a) for a in (
 683:                 raw["judge_critical_axes"] if "judge_critical_axes" in raw
 684:                 else raw.get("qwen_critical_axes", [])  # I-modref-004 (#530) legacy
 685:             )
 686:         ),
 687:         judge_parse_ok=bool(
 688:             raw["judge_parse_ok"] if "judge_parse_ok" in raw
 689:             else raw.get("qwen_parse_ok", False)  # I-modref-004 (#530) legacy
 690:         ),
 691:     )
 692: 
 693: 
 694: def _parse_retrieval_stats(raw: Any) -> RetrievalStats | None:
 695:     if not isinstance(raw, Mapping):
 696:         return None
 697:     api_calls = raw.get("api_calls", {})
 698:     if not isinstance(api_calls, Mapping):
 699:         api_calls = {}
 700:     by_provider: dict[str, int] = {}
 701:     for k, v in api_calls.items():
 702:         try:
 703:             by_provider[str(k)] = int(v)
 704:         except (TypeError, ValueError):
 705:             continue
 706:     queries_raw = raw.get("queries") or raw.get("query_log") or []
 707:     queries: list[str] = []
 708:     if isinstance(queries_raw, list):
 709:         for q in queries_raw:
 710:             if isinstance(q, str):
 711:                 queries.append(q)
 712:             elif isinstance(q, Mapping) and "query" in q:
 713:                 queries.append(str(q["query"]))
 714:     return RetrievalStats(
 715:         pre_filter=int(raw.get("pre_filter", 0)),
 716:         fetched=int(raw.get("fetched", 0)),
 717:         failed=int(raw.get("failed", 0)),
 718:         by_provider=MappingProxyType(by_provider),
 719:         queries=tuple(queries),
 720:     )
 721: 
 722: 
 723: def _parse_adequacy(raw: Any) -> AdequacyGate | None:
 724:     if not isinstance(raw, Mapping):
 725:         return None
 726:     return AdequacyGate(
 727:         decision=str(raw.get("decision", "")),
 728:         findings_ok=int(raw.get("findings_ok", 0)),
 729:         findings_total=int(raw.get("findings_total", 0)),
 730:         critical_count=int(raw.get("critical_count", 0)),
 731:     )
 732: 
 733: 
 734: def _parse_corpus_approval(raw: Any) -> CorpusApprovalGate | None:
 735:     """Load corpus_approval.json. Returns None if file is absent."""
 736:     if not isinstance(raw, Mapping):
 737:         return None
 738:     return CorpusApprovalGate(
 739:         approved=bool(raw.get("approved", False)),
 740:         decision_at_iso=str(raw.get("decision_at_iso", "")),
 741:         user_note=str(raw.get("user_note", "")),
 742:         approved_count=len(raw.get("approved_source_urls") or []),
 743:         rejected_count=len(raw.get("rejected_source_urls") or []),
 744:     )
 745: 
 746: 
 747: def _parse_completeness_percent(raw: Any) -> float:
 748:     """Compute completeness as a percentage, 0.0–100.0.
 749: 
 750:     V30 manifests use either:
 751:       - {covered_fraction: 0.0–1.0}
 752:       - {total_covered: int, total_applicable: int}
 753:       - older keys: {covered_topics, total_topics} or {covered, total}
 754: 
 755:     Codex M-1 review caught that the old code looked for keys that don't
 756:     exist in the V30 schema, returning 0.0 for a 7/7 manifest.
 757:     """
 758:     if not isinstance(raw, Mapping):
 759:         return 0.0
 760:     if "covered_fraction" in raw:
 761:         try:
 762:             return float(raw["covered_fraction"]) * 100.0
 763:         except (TypeError, ValueError):
 764:             pass
 765:     for cov_key, tot_key in (
 766:         ("total_covered", "total_applicable"),
 767:         ("covered_topics", "total_topics"),
 768:         ("covered", "total"),
 769:     ):
 770:         if cov_key in raw and tot_key in raw:
 771:             try:
 772:                 cov = float(raw[cov_key])
 773:                 tot = float(raw[tot_key])
 774:                 if tot > 0:
 775:                     return (cov / tot) * 100.0
 776:             except (TypeError, ValueError):
 777:                 continue
 778:     return 0.0
 779: 
 780: 
 781: def _parse_manifest(raw: Mapping[str, Any]) -> RunManifest:
 782:     _require_keys(
 783:         raw,
 784:         (
 785:             "run_id",
 786:             "slug",
 787:             "status",
 788:             "question",
 789:             "protocol_sha256",
 790:             "evaluator_gate",
 791:             "completeness",
 792:         ),
 793:         "manifest.json",
 794:     )
 795:     generator = raw.get("generator", {})
 796:     if not isinstance(generator, Mapping):
 797:         generator = {}
 798:     return RunManifest(
 799:         run_id=str(raw["run_id"]),
 800:         slug=str(raw["slug"]),
 801:         status=str(raw["status"]),
 802:         question=str(raw["question"]),
 803:         protocol_sha256=str(raw["protocol_sha256"]),
 804:         cost_usd=float(raw.get("cost_usd", 0.0)),
 805:         budget_cap_usd=float(raw.get("budget_cap_usd", 0.0)),
 806:         word_count=int(generator.get("words", 0)),
 807:         sentences_verified=int(generator.get("sentences_verified", 0)),
 808:         sentences_dropped=int(generator.get("sentences_dropped", 0)),
 809:         contradictions_found=int(raw.get("contradictions_found", 0)),
 810:         completeness_percent=_parse_completeness_percent(raw["completeness"]),
 811:         evaluator_gate=_parse_evaluator_gate(raw["evaluator_gate"]),
 812:         release_allowed=bool(raw.get("release_allowed", False)),
 813:         v30_enabled=bool(raw.get("v30_enabled", False)),
 814:         v30_warnings=tuple(str(w) for w in raw.get("v30_warnings", [])),
 815:         retrieval_stats=_parse_retrieval_stats(raw.get("retrieval")),
 816:     )
 817: 
 818: 
 819: def _parse_verification_token(raw: Mapping[str, Any]) -> EvidenceSpanToken:
 820:     return EvidenceSpanToken(
 821:         evidence_id=str(raw.get("evidence_id", "")),
 822:         start=int(raw.get("start", 0)),
 823:         end=int(raw.get("end", 0)),
 824:     )
 825: 
 826: 
 827: def _parse_verification_sentence(
 828:     raw: Mapping[str, Any], section_title: str, status: str, idx: int
 829: ) -> ReportSentence:
 830:     return ReportSentence(
 831:         claim_id=f"{section_title}:{status}:{idx}",
 832:         section=section_title,
 833:         text=str(raw.get("sentence", "")),
 834:         tokens=tuple(
 835:             _parse_verification_token(t) for t in raw.get("tokens", [])
 836:         ),
 837:         is_verified=(status == "kept"),
 838:         failure_reasons=tuple(str(r) for r in raw.get("failure_reasons", [])),
 839:     )

codex
Pytest itself is creating locked temp directories in this sandbox, so the focused suite cannot run here despite the repo code importing correctly. I’m doing a direct resolver smoke check instead: seed a run DB, create synthetic artifacts, and exercise the success, abort, release-blocked, and non-directory artifact cases without pytest’s temp fixture.

"C:\\Program Files\\PowerShell\\7\\pwsh.exe" -Command '$env:PYTHONPATH='"'src'; @'
from pathlib import Path
import json, os
from fastapi import HTTPException

from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
from polaris_v6.api.bundle import load_evidence_contract_for_run
from tests.polaris_v6.api.test_artifact_to_slice_chain import _write_synthetic_artifact_dir

root = Path(r'C:\\POLARIS\\codex_review_tmp\\manual_gate_test')
root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
db = root / 'runs.sqlite'
os.environ[run_store.ENV_DB_PATH] = str(db)
run_store.init_db(str(db))

def seed_completed(run_id, artifact_dir, status):
    run_store.insert_run(run_id, 'clinical', 'noop?', path=str(db))
    run_store.mark_in_progress(run_id, path=str(db))
    run_store.set_pipeline_meta(run_id, query_slug=run_id, artifact_dir=str(artifact_dir), path=str(db))
    run_store.mark_completed(run_id, {'manifest': {'status': status}, 'status': status}, pipeline_status=status, cost_usd=0.1, path=str(db))

def expect_http(label, fn):
    try:
        out = fn()
        print(f'{label}: 200 {type(out).__name__}')
    except HTTPException as exc:
        print(f'{label}: HTTP {exc.status_code}')

success_dir = _write_synthetic_artifact_dir(root / 'success_parent')
seed_completed('ok_run', success_dir, 'success')
expect_http('success', lambda: load_evidence_contract_for_run('ok_run'))

release_dir = _write_synthetic_artifact_dir(root / 'release_parent')
manifest_path = release_dir / 'manifest.json'
manifest = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
manifest['release_allowed'] = False
manifest['status'] = 'partial_evaluator_advisory'
manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(manifest), encoding='utf-8')
seed_completed('release_blocked', release_dir, 'partial_evaluator_advisory')
expect_http('release_blocked', lambda: load_evidence_contract_for_run('release_blocked'))

abort_dir = _write_synthetic_artifact_dir(root / 'abort_parent')
run_store.insert_run('abort_run', 'clinical', 'noop?', path=str(db))
run_store.mark_in_progress('abort_run', path=str(db))
run_store.set_pipeline_meta('abort_run', query_slug='abort_run', artifact_dir=str(abort_dir), path=str(db))
run_store.mark_aborted('abort_run', pipeline_status='abort_corpus_inadequate', abort_reason='test', cost_usd=0.1, path=str(db))
expect_http('abort', lambda: load_evidence_contract_for_run('abort_run'))

file_path = root / 'not_a_dir.txt'
file_path.write_text('not a dir', encoding='utf-8')
seed_completed('not_dir', file_path, 'success')
expect_http('not_dir', lambda: load_evidence_contract_for_run('not_dir'))
